***забирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забирать.html>забира́ть</a> (4105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-birátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забирать.html>забира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забрать.html>забра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take away, to seize, to collect; to capture, to take possession
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забирать.html>забира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabirátʹ</b> sebé v gólovu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take it into one's head</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to collect, to pick up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забирать.html>забира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabirátʹ</b> továr</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pick up the goods</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to arrest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>людьми́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приезжать.html>приезжа́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́нах</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:называемый.html>называ́емых</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:воронко.html>воро́нках</a>», <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ноча́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забирать.html>забира́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>це́лыми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:семья.html>се́мьями</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Za ljudʹmí prijezžáli na čórnyx mašínax, tak nazyvájemyx “vorónkax”, po nočám i <b>zabiráli</b> célymi sémʹjami.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They came for people in black cars, the so-called "voronkas" ("funnels") in the night and <b>arrested</b> entire families.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pick up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to collect a passenger</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забирать.html>забира́ю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сы́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>zabiráju</b> sýna pósle rabóty.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I pick up (my) son after work.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bear, to turn off, to aside
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забирать.html>забира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вправо.html>впра́во</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabirátʹ</b> vprávo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bear (to the) right</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>би<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рать.html>ра́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:забрать.html>забра́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-бир-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забить.html>заби́ть</a> (5986)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забить.html>заби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забивать.html>забива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive in (nail), to hammer in, to nail up</li>
<li>to score (a goal)</li>
<li>to beat up</li>
<li>to slaughter</li>
<li>to block up, to stop up, to cram, to obstruct</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to outdo, to surpass</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ignore, to neglect <span class="use-with-mention">something the actor is supposed to do</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stop doing something <span class="use-with-mention">especially because of one's couldn't care less attitude</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give up on one's (previous) intention</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reserve, to earmark</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:забиться.html>заби́ться</a> (6508)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забить.html>заби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забиться.html>заби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забиваться.html>забива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get clogged or blocked with</li>
<li>to hide, to get (into a corner)</li>
<li>to begin to beat/throb
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:забиться.html>заби́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>zabílosʹ</b> sérdce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his heart began to beat/throb/thump/thud/pound</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забить.html>заби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>би́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 11b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:забиваться.html>забива́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-би-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.

***заблаговременно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заблаговременно.html>заблаговре́менно</a> (21582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заблаговременно.html>заблаговре́менно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zablagovrémenno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>in due time, beforehand, in advance, ahead of time</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заранее.html>зара́нее</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaráneje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-благ-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-времен-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-н-о</b>.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>; has the form of a past active participle. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заболевание.html>заболева́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabolevánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заболевание.html>заболева́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заболевание.html>заболева́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заболевание.html>заболева́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>disease, sickness, illness
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1970</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>Наде́жда</a> Яковлевна Мандельштам (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nadezhda_Mandelstam" class="extiw" title="w:Nadezhda Mandelstam">Nadezhda Yakovlevna Mandelstam</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:воспоминание.html>Воспомина́ния</a></cite>, chapter 18, "<a href = vnd.unilang:профессия.html>Профе́ссия</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:болезнь.html>боле́знь</a> [Professional Sickness]", New York |  Chekhov Publishing House, page 74 |  translated as <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Max_Hayward" class="extiw" title="w:Max Hayward">Max Hayward</a>, transl., <cite>Hope Against Hope</cite>, New York |  Atheneum, 1970, page 70:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>ка́жется</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слуховой.html>слуховы́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:галлюцинация.html>галлюцина́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:являться.html>явля́ются</a> чем-то <a href = vnd.unilang:вроде.html>вро́де</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:профессиональный.html>профессиона́льного</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заболевание.html>заболева́ния</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne kážetsja, što dlja poéta sluxovýje galljucinácii javljájutsja čem-to vróde professionálʹnovo <b>zabolevánija</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I imagine that for a poet auditory hallucinations are something in the nature of an occupational <b>disease</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заболевать.html>заболева́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabolevájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заболевать.html>заболева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabolevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забор.html>забо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забор.html>забо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забор.html>забо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забор.html>забо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fence</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> intake
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забор.html>забо́р</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здуха</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabór</b> vózduxa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">air intake</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>collection
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:забор.html>забо́р</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:письменный.html>пи́сьменных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обращение.html>обраще́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zabór</b> písʹmennyx obraščénij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">collection of written requests</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">зобота</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zobota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***заботить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заботить.html>забо́тить</a> (19133)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забота.html>забо́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zabóta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заботить.html>забо́тить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zabótitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озаботить.html>озабо́тить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to worry, to be a cause for concern <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заботить.html>забо́тит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nas <b>zabótit</b> to, što</i> ― <span class="e-translation">we are concerned about the fact that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заботить.html>забо́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto jevó óčenʹ <b>zabótit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is very concerned [very much worried] about it</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пусть.html>пусть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заботить.html>забо́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pustʹ éto vas ne <b>zabótit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't concern yourself with it</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>мало</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заботить.html>забо́тит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto jevó malo <b>zabótit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he hardly cares; little does he care about it</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
